AUTHOR     (J.NEBE, G.J.KIROUAC)                                  2015700100009 
TITLE      -ELASTIC NEUTRON SCATTERING FROM CA-40 FOR NEUTRON     2015700100010 
            ENERGIES TO 2 MEV.-                                   2015700100011 
FACILITY   .KARLSRUHE ISOCHRONOUS CYCLOTRON.                      2015700100012 
INC-SOURCE .U-(D,NX) REACTION BY 40 MEV DEUTERONS.                2015700100013 
            A DEFLECTION SYSTEM PRODUCED NEUTRON BUNCHES OF ABOUT 2015700100014 
            1 NS DURATION AT A REPETITION RATE OF 19.13 KHZ,      2015700100015 
            NEUTRON FLUX ABOUT 3.E+4 N/CM2*SEC.  THE NEUTRON BEAM 2015700100016 
            WAS MONITORED BY A PULSE-SHAPE DISCRIMINATER DETECTOR.2015700100017 
INC-SPECT  .THE NEUTRON SPECTRUM FROM THE KARLSRUHE ISOCHRONOUS   2015700100018 
            CYCLOTRON SPECTROMETER IS A SMOOTH, SLOWLY VARYING    2015700100019 
            FUNCTION IN THE ENERGY REGION FROM 0.55 TO 2 MEV.     2015700100020 
SAMPLE     .A METALLIC CALCIUM CYLINDER, 5 CM DIAMETER            2015700100021 
            AND 12 CM LONG, ENCAPSULATED IN 50 MU SILVER FOIL,    2015700100022 
            THE THICKNESS = 0.09 ATOMS/BARNS.                     2015700100023 
           .THE SAMPLE PURITY BETTER THAN 99.5 PER CENT.          2015700100024 
           .FOR NORMALIZATION TO THE SCATTERING CROSS SECTION, A  2015700100025 
            HIGH PURITY (99.9 PER CENT) GRAPHITE SAMPLE WAS USED  2015700100026 
            IN THE FORM OF A HOLLOW CYLINDER WITH AN INNER DIA-   2015700100027 
            METER OF 2.5 CM AND THE SAME OUTER DIMENTIONS AS      2015700100028 
            CALCIUM SAMPLE.                                       2015700100029 
METHOD     (TOF  )    FLIGHT PATH = 58 M, OVERALL TIME RESOLUTION 2015700100030 
            IS 4 NS. (I.E. ENERGY RESOLUTION OF 700 EV AT 0.55 MEV2015700100031 
            AND 6.1 KEV AT 2 MEV).                                2015700100032 
DETECTOR   (SCIN )    THREE NE-102A PLASTIC SCINTILLATORS, 12.4 CM2015700100033 
            DIAMETER BY 2.5 CM THICK, MOUNTED ON VALVO XP-1040    2015700100034 
            PHOTO-MULTIPLIERS, AND FAST ANODE OUTPUT HAD A ZERO   2015700100035 
            CROSSOVER TUNNEL DIODE TIME MARK CIRCUIT.             2015700100036 
           .AS THE NEUTRON FLUX DETECTOR, A SMALL NE-102A         2015700100037 
            SCINTILLATOR (5 CM DIAMETER, 1.2 CM THICK) WAS USED.  2015700100038 
           .THE SYSTEM (4 NE-102A DETECTORS, A DETECTOR POSITION  2015700100039 
            CODER AND LEBEN UC-KB TIME ANALYSER) COUPLED TO A     2015700100040 
            CDC-3100 ON-LINE COMPUTER.                            2015700100041 
           .THE TOF SPECTRUM FOR EACH DETECTOR WAS TAKEN OVER A   2015700100042 
            RANGE OF 4 MICROSEC WITH CHANNEL WIDTHS OF 2NS.       2015700100043 
           .A NEUTRON BEAM MONITOR PLACED AT 6 DEG TO THE NEUTRON 2015700100044 
            BEAM AT A DISTANCE OF 11 M FROM THE SOURCE,           2015700100045 
           .BY ALUMINUM COLLIMATOR, 30 CM IN DIAMETER BY 1 M LONG,2015700100046 
            THE NEUTRON BEAM CONFINED TO 3.0 MICRO-STERADIAN AT   2015700100047 
            THE END OF THE 58 M FLIGHT PATH.                      2015700100048 
           .DATA WERE SIMULTANEOUSLY TAKEN AT LABORATORY ANGLES OF2015700100049 
            54, 90 AND 140 DEGREES BY 3 SCATTERING DETECTORS, AND 2015700100050 
            0 DEG FOR FLUX MONITORING (NE-102A).                  2015700100051 
MONITOR    (6-C-12(N,EL)6-C-12,,DA)                               2015700100052 
            LANGSDORF ET AL.,PHYS.REV.107(1957)1077.              2015700100053 
CORRECTION .CORRECTIONS WERE MADE FOR THE FINITE SCATTERING SAMPLE2015700100054 
            THICKNESS OF CA AND C MEASURED WITH SIMILAR ENERGY    2015700100055 
            RESOLUTION AT THE KIC SPECTROMETER, IN THE CALCULATION2015700100056 
            OF THE CROSS SECTION.  THE CORRECTION WAS SMALL FOR   2015700100057 
            THIN CA SAMPLE BUT WAS ABOUT 20 PER CENT FOR C DATA,  2015700100058 
            NO CORRECTIONS WERE MADE FOR MULTIPLE SCATTERING.     2015700100059 
           .BACK GROUND COUNTING RATES IN THE OPEN BEAM SPECTRUM  2015700100060 
            WERE LESS THAN 5 PER CENT OF THE SAMPLE OUT COUNTING  2015700100061 
            RATE ABOVE 1 MEV. BELOW THIS ENERGY THE FRACTION      2015700100062 
            INCREASED TO 15 PER CENT.                             2015700100063 
ERR-ANALYS .WITH AN INCIDENT NEUTRON FLUX (ABOUT 3.E+4 N/CM2*SEC),2015700100064 
            A COUNTING STATISTICS OF 2 PER CENT WAS ACHIEVED IN   2015700100065 
            MOST OF THE 2048 TIME CHANNELS FOR EACH DETECTOR IN   2015700100066 
            100 H OF RUNNIG TIME.                                 2015700100067 
           .THE STATISTICAL ERROR IS GIVEN AS 3 PERCENT AND AFTER 2015700100068 
            NORMALIZING TO THE CARBON, THE ABSOLUTE CROSS SECTION 2015700100069 
            VALUES ARE ESTIMATED TO HAVE LESS THAN 15 PER CENT    2015700100070 
            UNCERTAINTY.                                          2015700100071 
COMMENT    .THE PRIMARY PURPOSE OF THE WORK WAS TO ASSIGN SPINS   2015700100072 
            AND PARITIES (L-VALUES) FOR CA40(N,N) RESONANCES BY   2015700100073 
            THE RESONANCE SHAPES AND SYMMETRY PROPERTIES.  PRECISE2015700100074 
            ABSOLUTE VALUES FOR THE CA-40 DIFFERENTIAL SCATTERING 2015700100075 
            CROSS SECTION WERE NOT THE PRINCIPAL CONCERN.         2015700100076
